20.6(1): gnas sku/ lha rgyal ma brtsal lhun grub sku/ bon nyid dbyings las ye shes g.yos/
20.7(1): ye shes rtsal las rdzogs skur shar/ mtshan dper 'dzom pas longs spyod rdzogs/ lha 
20.8(1): lngas bdud lnga gnas su dag /ye shes lnga yis dug lnga 'joms/ rigs lngas nyon 
20.9(1): mongs gnas su sbyangs/ sku lngas phung po dbyings su spar/ spyan lngas sems can 
20.10(1): thugs rjes gzigs/ yul snang dbyings kyi yum du shar/ rig shes nam mkha'i yab 
20.11(1): tu sprul/ 'khor ni sems dpa' sems mar bcas/ 'phrin las lnga yis 'od zer 
20.12(1): 'gyed/ 'gro 'dul sprul sku grangs med spros/ bgegs 'dul za byed rngam par 
20.13(1): 'gyed/ spa bkong mnyam pa'i zhi tshul ston/ 'gro 'dul gshen rab grangs med sprul/
20.14(1): sku yi gnas dang thugs rje las/ lkugs pa kha 'byed yi ge spros/ sum cu rtsa dgus 
20.15(1): go phyes nas/ rgyud lung man ngag grangs su 'chad/ mdo 'bum gzungs sde'i bka' 
20.16(1): 'chad nas/ mtha' yas sems can bde la bkod/ dbyings las ye shes g.yos 
20.17(1): tshul lo/ /bon nyid rdzogs skur sprul tshul lo/ /'khor rnams sems kyis dang bar

20.21(1): 7 de nas yang rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ston pa gshen rab kyis/ 'khor 
21.1(1): gyi gshen rab g.yung drung sems dpa' rnams la bka' stsal pa/ bon nyid dbyings 
21.2(1): nas thugs rje g.yos/ rdzogs pa'i sku las sprul skur sprul/ bskal pa'i lha gshen 
21.3(1): srid pa yis/ sems can thams cad 'dren par 'gyur/ zhes bka' bstsal to/ /de 
21.4(1): nas gto bu 'bum sangs kyis/ bla gos 'phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ me tog 
21.5(1): 'thor zhing bskor ba byas/ lha phyag btsal nas zhus pa'i mdo/ kye thugs rje'i stobs 
21.6(1): kyis bskal pa'i sems can 'dren/ bskal srid grangs med mkhyen pa'i gshen rab

21.10(1): lags/ zhes zhus sam gsol to/ /

21.13(1): de/ bdag ni skye ba 'di yi yang gong du/ srid pa ye sangs yul du ni/ gto rgyal
